      • addAsBusCentres

        public void addAsBusCentres(java.lang.CharSequence param)
        Appends the specified AsBusCentres to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates those countries whose calendars must be checked with regard to holiday (working day) validation. The default value will be the Country of the currency of the Asset side of the contract, but additional Country codes can be manually input if required. For example, the country codes of the participants and/or the Liability leg. Validation Rules: 2 Alpha characters. (Optional input. Multi-valued field). The code must be a a valid definition on the COUNTRY table and must have a valid entry on the REGION/HOLIDAY table. Defaulted to the Country of the Asset leg Currency.

        Parameters:
        param - the AsBusCentres to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addAsInterestDet

        public void addAsInterestDet(TField param)
        Appends the specified AsInterestDet to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The interest details of the asset leg of the swap transaction are stored here. This field will only be used when the assest leg is floating, and is used when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record does not hold sufficient detail for the generation of the SWIFT message. In this case the value 'OTHER' is used in field 14F on the SWIFT message and the value in this field is used. This field will not be used if the asset leg is fixed. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record specified in the field AS.RATE.KEY has a rate text which does not correspond to the format alpha / alpha / alpha. Refer to the helptext on field RATE.TEXT on the file MARKET.RATE.TEXT A maximum of six multi values are allowed for this field.

        Parameters:
        param - the AsInterestDet to append
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void addEntryIds(TField param)
        Appends the specified EntryIds to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Multi-valued field which identifies the entries raised by the contract. The entry Ids are generated automatically by the system and identify either a statement entry or a category entry in respect of the contract. The number automatically generated is unique to the associated contract and is built in the following way : Eg. 673732684.48 o The first four digits "6737" indicates the number of days since the 1st of January 1968. o The next five "32684" indicates the number of seconds since midnight. o The last two digits "48" indicates the number of hundreds of seconds. Validation Rules: 29 Alphanumeric characters. (No-input. System generated).

      • getAccountOfficer

        public TField getAccountOfficer()

      • getActionType

        public TField getActionType()
        Returns the ActionType

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository. Under the Regulatory Reporting to a Trade Repository, it is not only the initial trade that is reported but also the life cycle events of the Trade that follow. A change in the action type is indicative of an event on the contract and requires to be reported. Change in Action Types is allowed both manually and automatically. Specifies the ACTION.TYPE that is populated based on the event on trade. Input to this field is allowed only when OC module is installed. Validation Rules: Allowed optional values are N, M, E, C, Z, O, R and P N denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is NEW. Value of 'N' is defaulted for a new contract. User is also allowed to change the status to N if the previous status is E. E denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is REVERSE or Correction. In case of wrongly entered UTI values or a Temporary UTI was used previously, the old UTI should be reported with ACTION.TYPE as 'E' for error reporting first and then change the Action Type to NEW after keying in the actual UTI. This way the previous reporting with temporary UTI is replaced by the one with final UTI. Action Type E is also used to undo the reporting of a particular transaction done which should not have been done reported at all in the first instance. M denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is MODIFIED. In case of change in the RATE.FIXING.DATE the ACTION.TYPE is set to 'M'. C denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is CANCELLED. In case of any change in maturity/value date i.e. early termination of the contract should be reported with C. In FRA this MATURITY.DATE field is No change field. So ACTION.TYPE never gets populated automatically with type as C but It can be manually updated as c and the contract can be cancelled. Z denotes Compression update. This means the trade being reported is generated out of a compression activity. O denotes OTHER types. When OTHER is used, additional information as to what OTHER mean should be mentioned separately.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The ActionType

      • getAgreementType

        public TField getAgreementType()
        Returns the AgreementType

        Field description: Defines the swap contract Agreement type. If a matster agreement type is entered then the default full agreement type (eg TYPE / DATE // VERSION) will be used on the SWAP contract if such an agreement type has been entered on the master SWAP.AGREEMENT.TYPE record. Eg. ISDA (International Swap Dealers Association), BBAIRS, MASTER, etc. This is also used to define Swift Message conditions. Corresponds to field 77 on Swift messages. Validation Rules: 1-12 Alphanumeric characters. (Mandatory input). Must be a valid definition on the SWAP.AGREEMENT.TYPE file. Each contract must be linked to an agreement type.

      • getAsBasis

        public TField getAsBasis()
        Returns the AsBasis

        Field description: Defines the Interest Day Basis which indicates the calculation method to be used for interest amount calculations on the asset leg. Input can be any valid basis type defined on the INTEREST.BASIS table. Eg. Basis Calculation method signified ===== ============================ A 360/360 A2 30/360 B 366/360 C Act/Act (ISDA) C2 Act/Act (AFB) D 360/366 E 366/365 E1 365/365 F 360/365 F2 30/365 S SPECIAL Validation Rules: 1-10 Alphanumeric characters. (Mandatory input). The Basis type entered must be a valid key on the INTEREST.BASIS table. Defaulted to the Interest Day Basis specified on the CURRENCY file for the Asset currency (AS.CURRENCY). For Basis type 'S' the INTEREST amount will be Mandatory. Also FIXED.RATE and RATE.KEY are not allowed.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsBasis

        public TField getAsCurTrsryRate()

      • getAsCurrency

        public TField getAsCurrency()
        Returns the AsCurrency

        Field description: Indicates the currency of the asset side of the swap contract. This field indicates the currency of the asset side of the swap contract and will be the same as the currency of the various accounts where the accounting movements in respect of the contract will be debited or credited. Validation Rules: 3 type SSS (uppercase alpha) characters. or 1-3 numeric character currency code. (Optional input; Default = local currency). The currency code must exist on the CURRENCY table. Any existing currency code will be accepted and the name redisplayed for checking. Once the contract has been authorised this field cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsCurrency

      • getAsCurrentRate

        public TField getAsCurrentRate()
        Returns the AsCurrentRate

        Field description: Specifies the interest rate for the current interest period of the Swap asset leg. This field contains the current rate of interest to be used when accruing interest on the outstanding balance of the asset side of the contract. This field is a no-input field and is defaulted via : o The fixed interest rate (AS.FIXED.RATE) or, o The combined/calculated floating interest rate using AS.RATE.KEY and AS.SPREAD This rate can only be changed by defining and processing a Rate Reset schedule (type "RR") on the contract. Validation Rules: 1-11 numeric characters. (No-input field). If the current rate is not greater than zero, an override message is set.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsCurrentRate

      • getAsDateAdjustment

        public TField getAsDateAdjustment()
        Returns the AsDateAdjustment

        Field description: Defines the type of date adjustments that are to be followed on the Asset leg. Depending on the date adjustment, the process date of the schedules and the interest effective dates are calculated. Valid date adjustments and their effects are as follows : DATE.ADJUSTMENT ENTRY.DATE EFFECTIVE.DATE =============== ========== ============== o null SCHEDULE.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o VALUE PROCESS.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o PERIOD PROCESS.DATE PROCESS.DATE Where, ENTRY.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Date Adjustment specified (AS.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). EFFECTIVE.DATE is the end date of the current interest period determined by the Date Adjustment specified (AS.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). SCHEDULE.DATE is the date of the schedule as specified in the swap contract (AS.DATE.FREQ). PROCESS.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Asset Day Convention (AS.DAY.CONVENTION). Validation Rules: 1-6 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Must be set to either "null", "VALUE", or "PERIOD".

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsDateAdjustment

      • getAsDayConvention

        public TField getAsDayConvention()
        Returns the AsDayConvention

        Field description: Defines the Day Convention to follow. Based on the Day Convention (AS.DAY.CONVENTION) and the Business Centres (AS.BUS.CENTRES) the process date of the Asset leg schedules are determined. Valid Day Conventions are as follows : o null the process date is the date of the schedule. o FOLLOWING the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule. o MODIFIED the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule providing this date does not fall into the next calendar month. In which case the process date is the first preceding business day. o PRECEDING the process date is the first preceding business day. Validation Rules: 1-10 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Valid Day Conventions are either "null", "FOLLOWING", "PRECEDING", or "MODIFIED".

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsDayConvention

      • getAsFixedInterest

        public TField getAsFixedInterest()
        Returns the AsFixedInterest

        Field description: Specifies whether the current interest amount payments on the asset leg are of a fixed or floating amount. This field is a no-input field and is set to either "Y" for fixed interest amounts, and "NO" (default) for floating interest amounts. This field is determined by the interest payment schedules ("IP") defined on the Asset side of the contract. o If the IP schedule (AS.TYPE) has an amount specified (AS.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "Y". o If the IP schedule (AS.TYPE) does not have an amount specified (AS.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "NO". Validation Rules: 1-2 Alpha characters. "Y" signifies a fixed interest amount for the current period. "NO" signifies a floating interest amount for the current period. (No-input field. Default = "NO").

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsFixedInterest

      • getAsFixedRate

        public TField getAsFixedRate()
        Returns the AsFixedRate

        Field description: Specifies the fixed interest rate at which interest is to be accrued on the Asset leg. Once the contract has been drawn down, ie. the contract status is "CUR", this field cannot be changed. However, the interest rate can be changed at any time via the definition of a Rate Reset ("RR") schedule. Validation Rules: 1-11 numeric characters. (Optional Input). Input is prohibited if data is present in the fields AS.RATE.KEY and AS.SPREAD. A rate must be present in this field if the fields AS.RATE.KEY and AS.SPREAD are null. Field will be no-input once the contract has reached the Interest effective date, ie. contract status = "CUR".

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsFixedRate

      • getAsIntEffective

        public TField getAsIntEffective()
        Returns the AsIntEffective

        Field description: Identifies the start date of the first interest period and therefore the true Value date of the Asset leg. It is the date on which interest accruals commence on the outstanding balance of the contract. This date can be entered as either the current date (today) or a date in the past (less than the contract value date). It cannot be greater than the contract value date. If forward dated, ie. both the value date and interest effective date are forward, then the contract status will be null until the effective date is reached, at which time, the principal amount will be drawn down and the contract status changed to "CUR". An input of a null value will result in the date being defaulted to the contract value date. If backdated or 'today' dated then the contract will be drawn down, put on-line, and the contract status set to "CUR". If backdated into a prior month, interest will be accrued on-line up to the end of the previous month. Input of a non working day will require an override. Validation Rules: Standard Date format. Defaults to the contract Value Date. Cannot be greater than the contract Value Date. Input is prohibited was the contract status has been set to "CUR" (Current). An override will be required if this date is a non-working day.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AsIntEffective

In this case the value 'OTHER' is used in field 14F on the SWIFT message and the value in this field is used. This field will not be used if the asset leg is fixed. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record specified in the field AS.RATE.KEY has a rate text which does not correspond to the format alpha / alpha / alpha. Refer to the helptext on field RATE.TEXT on the file MARKET.RATE.TEXT A maximum of six multi values are allowed for this field.

        Field description: Indicates the spread (also known as the margin) which will be applied to the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. The subtraction of the INTEREST SPREAD from the INTEREST KEY must be specifically indicated by the insertion of the '-' (minus) sign in front of the INTEREST SPREAD. Validation Rules: Upto 11 numeric characters plus a decimal point. A minus sign has to be placed in front if the spread is to be deducted from the INTEREST KEY. Input is optional when a rate key has been define, ie. AS.RATE.KEY, otherwise input is not allowed. (Default value = null) Input in this field is only allowed for contracts when a rate key has been specified, ie. AS.RATE.KEY is not null.

      • getBalanceSheet

        public TField getBalanceSheet()
        Returns the BalanceSheet

        Field description: This field details whether the SWAP contract is to be treated as an ON balance sheet instrument or an OFF balance sheet instrument. This value is defaulted from the SWAP.TYPE of the swap contract. When this field contains the value OFF the contract will undergo the currency revaluation processing. Each night each leg of the contract id revalued against the local currency if 1) The leg is not notional (ie the NOTIONAL field on the SWAP.BALANCES file is set to NO). 2) The currency of the leg is not the local currency. And any difference between this value and the value as of last night is posted as unreleasied profit and loss to the category specified on the SWAP.PARAMETER record. When this field contains the value of ON the contract will not be revalued. Validation Rules: Must contain either ON or OFF, which is set from the SWAP.TYPE. Input is not allowed to this field.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The BalanceSheet

      • getBaseCurrency

        public TField getBaseCurrency()
        Returns the BaseCurrency

        Field description: Identifies the base currency of the contract and will be used to verify the exchange rate. When the Base Currency is not specified and the transaction involves local Currency, the System will default to the local Currency provided that the Quotation code of the other Currency is NULL. If this is not the case (the Quotation code of the other Currency is not equal to null) then the other Currency will become the default. When the base Currency is not specified and the transaction involves two currencies where none is the Local Currency, it will default to the Currency which yields a cross-rate greater than unity (One). Please refer to Forex for more details. Validation Rules: 3 characters currency code (uppercase alpha or numeric) - Type SSS (Optional input. See details for default.) The currency entered must appear on the Currency table. The currency must be the same as either the asset or liability currency. Proper verification of the exchange rate will be performed by the system against the Exchange Rate values contained in the Currency table. When the Swap contract involves the local currency and the quotation code on the Foreign currency is equal to or greater than '0' (zero), the base currency can only be the Foreign Currency. Once authorised the Base currency cannot be amended.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The BaseCurrency

      • getCurrencyMarket

        public TField getCurrencyMarket()
        Returns the CurrencyMarket

        Field description: Identifies which Currency Market is accessed for this transaction. The use of this field will only be applicable for those countries where the exchange authorities have defined different markets for foreign currency dealing. A typical example would be Belgium where foreign currencies are dealt with on the Regular Market and also on the Free Market. The default value of '1' means that, for the majority of countries, where only one exchange rate market exists, input in this field will not be necessary. Note: In the present release, only one market can be defined on the CURRENCY.MARKET table. Consequently, for the time being, only the value of '1' will be accepted in this field. Validation Rules: One Numeric digit Currency Market code. (No input. System value is 1.) Any input in this field must be a valid code on the CURRENCY.MARKET table.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The CurrencyMarket

      • getCustomer

        public TField getCustomer()
        Returns the Customer

        Field description: Identifies the counterparty with whom the Bank makes the contract. This is the identification assigned to the Customer on first contact with the bank. The customer will be referred to by this identification in all subsequent operations with the Bank. The system will make use of this number to: a) Identify the Counterparty of the transaction engaged in by the Bank, b) Print the Customer's name and address on all contracts and/or advices produced by this module, c) Locate the liability number for limit checking on Placement contracts. Validation Rules: 3-10 alphanumeric customer mnemonic or, 1-10 numeric character customer number. (Mandatory input). Must be a valid Customer number or mnemonic. Once the contract has been authorised, this field cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The Customer

      • getFttCollCptyTax

        public TField getFttCollCptyTax()
        Returns the FttCollCptyTax

        Field description: Provides the option to T24 bank to collect the Financial Transaction Tax payable by the Counterparty also. If yes, accounting entries are raised to collect counterpartys tax wherein customer Account is debited and Tax suspense Account is credited. The values No or Null means T24 bank does not collect the FTT payable by the counterparty or in other words the counterparty himself remits the FTT. This option is provided on the premise that where the counterparty is a customer of the bank ( not an interbank counterparty) the T24 bank assumes responsibility to collect and pay the FTT payable by the customer Validation Rules: Values allowed are Yes, No or Null. Default value will be from SWAP.PARAMETER but can be overridden by the User.

      • getLbDateAdjustment

        public TField getLbDateAdjustment()
        Returns the LbDateAdjustment

        Field description: Defines the type of date adjustments that are to be followed on the Liability leg. Depending on the date adjustment, the process date of the schedules and the interest effective dates are calculated. Valid date adjustments and their effects are as follows : DATE.ADJUSTMENT ENTRY.DATE EFFECTIVE.DATE =============== ========== ============== o null SCHEDULE.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o VALUE PROCESS.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o PERIOD PROCESS.DATE PROCESS.DATE Where, ENTRY.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Date Adjustment specified (LB.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). EFFECTIVE.DATE is the end date of the current interest period determined by the Date Adjustment specified (LB.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). SCHEDULE.DATE is the date of the schedule as specified in the swap contract (LB.DATE.FREQ). PROCESS.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Asset Day Convention (LB.DAY.CONVENTION). Validation Rules: 1-6 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Must be set to either "null", "VALUE", or "PERIOD".

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LbDateAdjustment

      • getLbDayConvention

        public TField getLbDayConvention()
        Returns the LbDayConvention

        Field description: Defines the Day Convention to follow. Based on the Day Convention (LB.DAY.CONVENTION) and the Business Centres (LB.BUS.CENTRES) the process date of the Liability leg schedules are determined. Valid Day Conventions are as follows : o null the process date is the date of the schedule. o FOLLOWING the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule. o MODIFIED the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule providing this date does not fall into the next calendar month. In which case the process date is the first preceding business day. o PRECEDING the process date is the first preceding business day. Validation Rules: 1-10 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Valid Day Conventions are either "null", "FOLLOWING", "PRECEDING", or "MODIFIED".

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LbDayConvention

      • getLbFixedInterest

        public TField getLbFixedInterest()
        Returns the LbFixedInterest

        Field description: Specifies whether the current interest amount payments on the liability leg are of a fixed or floating amount. This field is a no-input field and is set to either "Y" for fixed interest amounts, and "NO" (default) for floating interest amounts. This field is determined by the interest payment schedules ("IP") defined on the Asset side of the contract. o If the IP schedule (LB.TYPE) has an amount specified (LB.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "Y". o If the IP schedule (LB.TYPE) does not have an amount specified (LB.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "NO". Validation Rules: 1-2 Alpha characters. "Y" signifies a fixed interest amount for the current period. "NO" signifies a floating interest amount for the current period. (No-input field. Default = "NO").

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LbFixedInterest

      • getLbIntEffective

        public TField getLbIntEffective()
        Returns the LbIntEffective

        Field description: Identifies the start date of the first interest period and therefore the true Value date of the Liability leg. It is the date on which interest accruals commence on the outstanding balance of the contract. This date can be entered as either the current date (today) or a date in the past (less than the contract value date). It cannot be greater than the contract value date. If forward dated, ie. both the value date and interest effective date are forward, then the contract status will be null until the effective date is reached, at which time, the principal amount will be drawn down and the contract status changed to "CUR". An input of a null value will result in the date being defaulted to the contract value date. If backdated or 'today' dated then the contract will be drawn down, put on-line, and the contract status set to "CUR". If backdated into a prior month, interest will be accrued on-line up to the end of the previous month. Input of a non working day will require an override. Validation Rules: Standard Date format. Defaults to the contract Value Date. Cannot be greater than the contract Value Date. Input is prohibited was the contract status has been set to "CUR" (Current). An override will be required if this date is a non-working day.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LbIntEffective

In this case the value 'OTHER' is used in field 14F on the SWIFT message and the value in this field is used. This field will not be used if the liability leg is fixed. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record specified in the field LB.RATE.KEY has a rate text which does not correspond to the format alpha / alpha / alpha. Refer to the helptext on field RATE.TEXT on the file MARKET.RATE.TEXT A maximum of six multi values are allowed for this field.

        public TField getLbSpread()
        Returns the LbSpread

        Field description: Indicates the spread (also known as the margin) which will be applied to the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. Note : T24 allows the user to define, on Floating rate contracts, a spread which can be added to or subtracted from the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. The subtraction of the INTEREST SPREAD from the INTEREST KEY must be specifically indicated by the insertion of the '-' (minus) sign in front of the INTEREST SPREAD. Validation Rules: Upto 11 numeric characters plus a decimal point. A minus sign has to be placed in front if the spread is to be deducted from the INTEREST KEY. Input is optional when a rate key has been define, ie. LB.RATE.KEY, otherwise input is not allowed. (Default value = null) Input in this field is only allowed for contracts when a rate key has been specified, ie. LB.RATE.KEY is not null.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LbSpread

      • getLbTrsyFixedRate

        public TField getLbTrsyFixedRate()
        Returns the LbTrsyFixedRate

        Field description: Specifies the treasury interest rate for the Liability leg. Once the contract has been drawn down, ie. the contract status is "CUR", this field cannot be changed. However, the interest rate can be changed at any time via the definition of a Rate Reset ("RR") schedule. Validation Rules: 1-11 numeric characters. (Optional Input). Input is prohibited if data is present in the fields LB.RATE.KEY and LB.SPREAD and TREASURY.CUSTOMER is not set as NO.. A rate must be present in this field if the fields LB.RATE.KEY and LB.SPREAD are null. Field will be no-input once the contract has reached the Interest effective date, ie. contract status = "CUR".

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LbTrsyFixedRate

      • getLimitReference

        public TField getLimitReference()
        Returns the LimitReference

        Field description: Identifies the LIMIT REFERENCE number to be checked for Limit control on transactions. Specifies the Credit Line number under which the transaction was granted. If no input is made in this field, then the Limits system will provide a default value according to the Limit Reference record which has its field application identifier set tyo "SW". If no match is found in selective Reference, the default value will be the Reference with its field reference blank. The credit line number generated will be NNNN-01 where NNNN is the Id of the Limit Reference record described above. Validation Rules: 3 - 10 numeric character LIMIT REFERENCE code. (Optional Input. Default value). Input in this field must be a valid LIMIT REFERENCE number. If no Limit exists for the counterparty a corresponding error message will be displayed by the system with an override facility. If the transaction amount exceeds the availability amount of the Limit, a corresponding error message will be displayed with an override facility.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LimitReference

      • getLinkReference

        public TField getLinkReference()
        Returns the LinkReference

        Field description: Defines the Transaction link reference of the Swap contract. The TRANS.LINK.REFERENCE file enables transactions to be linked together for reporting purposes. Eg. A Swap contract to a backing Loans and Deposits contract. The updating of the file is fully automatic : o If the user enters a reference id that does not exist on the reference file, a new record is created, and the contract Id concerned is held. o If the user changes the reference id, the contract Id concerned is moved to the new reference record. Should no other contracts exist on the reference, then that reference is removed. Validation Rules: 1-12 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input).

        Parameters:

      • getLiquidationMode

        public TField getLiquidationMode()
        Returns the LiquidationMode

        Field description: This field identifies the manner in which overdue payments are handled. The default for all contracts is AUTOMATIC. There are three options available: AUTOMATIC SEMI-AUTOMATIC MANUAL AUTOMATIC will liquidate across the settlement accounts on the contract. MANUAL will create a PD contract instead. SEMI-AUTOMATIC will only raise a PD contract if insufficient funds exist on the settlement account. For further details see the helptext in PD.PARAMETER where these settings are controlled from. Validation Rules: If the PD product is not installed for the current company then the only allowed setting is AUTOMATIC. Only AUTOMATIC allowed for liability contract types.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The LiquidationMode

      • getMatPaymentDate

        public TField getMatPaymentDate()
        Returns the MatPaymentDate

        Field description: Specifies whether the value date (Payment date) for the schedules that fall on the maturity date should be updated with the next working day of the deal currency when the maturity date of the Swap contract is a holiday. This functionality will be applicable only for the schedules that fall on the maturity date, provided DAY.CONVENTION is set as Following/ Modified. In case of Modified, if the last day of the month is a non-working day, then the value date will be the previous working day (as per PRECEDING). Irrespective of the input given in the field DATE.ADJUSTMENT (PERIOD or VALUE), System treats this as VALUE for the schedules falling on the maturity date, when the DAY.CONVENTION is set as Following/ Modified (excepting month end scenario). The new functionality of populating the value date will be applicable only when the field is set to YES. Validation Rules: : Input in this field is allowed only when the field MAT.PAYMENT.DATE in SWAP.PARAMETER is set to 'YES'. 'YES','NO' and NONE are the proposed values This field will be defaulted to YES if the field MAT.PAYMENT.DATE in SWAP.PARAMETER is set to 'YES' No input field after first authorisation

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The MatPaymentDate

      • getMaturityDate

        public TField getMaturityDate()
        Returns the MaturityDate

        Field description: Identifies when the swap contract is due to terminate. This field represents the latter date of when the principals are re-exchanged as scheduled, (AS/LB.TYPE = RX,CM) or when the final interest payment is made. The asset and liability dates for the re-exchange of principals or interest payments may not always be the same. The Maturity Date is the date on which the deal will be liquidated. At liquidation, all the corresponding amounts of principal (if appropriate) and interest will be passed to the appropriate accounts as designated within the transaction. Validation Rules: Type DD (standard date format in range 1000 - 2049) or, 3 numeric characters representing a number of days: (Mandatory input) The date will be checked against the HOLIDAY table. Any non-working day will require an override prior to acceptance. The maturity date must be greater than the value date. This date cannot be changed after authorisation when INTEREST BASIS = 'S' (Special). For Asset type contract, an override will be required when this date is smaller than the EXPIRY DATE of the corresponding Credit line.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The MaturityDate

      • getOcClgStatus

        public TField getOcClgStatus()
        Returns the OcClgStatus

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository. Denotes the OC Clearing Status. Input to this field is allowed only when OC module is installed. Validation Rules: Allowed optional values are Bilateral, Submitted, Accepted, Rejected, Cleared and Terminated. BILATERAL - when a fresh contract is inputted this field should be updated as BILATERAL. The previous status should be null. SUBMITTED - when the inputted contract is submitted to Trade Repository it should get updated as SUBMITTED.The previous clearing status of the contract should be BILATERAL. when OC.CLG.STATUS of the contract is SUBMITTED both CLG.MEM.ID and CENTRAl.CLG.PARTY fields cannot be NULL. ACCEPTED - when the contract is accepted by the Trade Repository it should get updated as ACCEPTED.The previous status should be SUBMITTED REJECTED - when the contract is rejected by the Trade Repository it should get updated as REJECTED.The previous status should be SUBMITTED CLEARED - When the status of the contract is ACCEPTED, User is expected to reverse the contract and enter a new one with Trade status as CLEARED.When the status is CLEARED, fields like CENTRAL.CLG.PARTY, CLG.MEM.ID, BILATERAL.REF are mandatory. Terminated - A cleared contract when cancelled/terminated by the Trade Repository should be updated as TERMINATED.The previous status should be CLEARED. This is a no change field.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The OcClgStatus

      • getTreasuryCustomer

        public TField getTreasuryCustomer()
        Returns the TreasuryCustomer

        Field description: The field will either hold values NULL or NO. By default it will hold NULL value, meaning that the customer in the deal is a treasury customer. It can be set to NO at the input level, wherein the interest rate charged to the customer is different from the treasury interest rate. Once this field is set to NO, then it becomes mandatory to input the treasury interest rate in the asset or liability side or both. When both the asset and liability side interest rate is set to floating, then TREASURY.CUSTOMER cannot be set to NO.The value in the field cannot be changed from NULL to NO or vice versa after authorization of the SWAP contract. The following input will be allowed in this field: 'NULL' = which means that the CPARTYof the deal is a Treasury Customer. 'NO' = which means that the CPARTYof the deal is not a Treasury Customer. (Optional input; default value = Null, i.e. the CPARTY is a Treasury Customer.)

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The TreasuryCustomer

      • getUniTranId

        public TField getUniTranId()
        Returns the UniTranId

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository All Trades should have a Unique Transaction Identifier (UTI) which is generated, communicated and matched Determination of who generates the UTI should follow the existing industry best practices for that Asset class The UTI.USI.API attached in OC.PARAMETER and invoked during FRA deal capture determines who is the party responsible for UTI generation and does the following. If a value is present during deal capture the API is not invoked, on the assumption that the UTI is generated and supplied by the other Counterparty. If no value is present during the deal capture, the API is invoked to determine the party responsible for generating the UTI. If the Other counterparty is responsible, still an UTI is generated with a suffix as TEMP to show that the UTI from the other counterparty is awaited and in the meantime, the reporting is done with a Temporary ID. If T24 Bank is responsible for UTI generation, then the same is generated without TEMP. Where a reporting has been made with UTI having TEMP as suffix and subsequently the Counterparty supplies the UTI, the following procedure has to be followed to ensure reporting with actual UTI. The field Action Type needs to be changed to E and record to be authorized. Later, the UTI field should be modified with the actual UTI received. Set the Action Type field to N and authorize the record. In this way, the previous reporting gets cancelled and the new reporting goes with correct UTI. Input to this field is allowed only when OC module is installed. Validation Rules : can contain up to 52 alphanumeric characters

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The UniTranId

      • getValueDate

        public TField getValueDate()
        Returns the ValueDate

        Field description: Contains the value date of the contract and is therefore the date from which the system will start to accrue interest. This date must be prior to the Maturity Date of the Contract such that the system may calculate interest. Validation Rules: Type DD (standard date format in range 1000 - 2049). (Optional input; Default value = Run date). The system will automatically access the HOLIDAY table to ensure that the value date is a working day and not a holiday in the country associated to the currency of the contract. Any Holiday will require an override.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The ValueDate

      • getVariationMarginPosted

        public TField getVariationMarginPosted()
        Returns the VariationMarginPosted

        Field description: This field holds the Value of the variation margin posted, including cash settled, by the reporting counterparty to the other counterparty. Where variation margin is posted on a portfolio basis, this field would indicate the overall value of variation margin posted for the portfolio. Validation Rules: Field is inputtable only if OC module is enabled

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The VariationMarginPosted

        public void insertAsBusCentres(TField param, int pos)
        Insert the specified AsBusCentres to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates those countries whose calendars must be checked with regard to holiday (working day) validation. The default value will be the Country of the currency of the Asset side of the contract, but additional Country codes can be manually input if required. For example, the country codes of the participants and/or the Liability leg. Validation Rules: 2 Alpha characters. (Optional input. Multi-valued field). The code must be a a valid definition on the COUNTRY table and must have a valid entry on the REGION/HOLIDAY table. Defaulted to the Country of the Asset leg Currency.

      • insertAsInterestDet

        public void insertAsInterestDet(TField param, int pos)
        Insert the specified AsInterestDet to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The interest details of the asset leg of the swap transaction are stored here. This field will only be used when the assest leg is floating, and is used when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record does not hold sufficient detail for the generation of the SWIFT message. In this case the value 'OTHER' is used in field 14F on the SWIFT message and the value in this field is used. This field will not be used if the asset leg is fixed. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record specified in the field AS.RATE.KEY has a rate text which does not correspond to the format alpha / alpha / alpha. Refer to the helptext on field RATE.TEXT on the file MARKET.RATE.TEXT A maximum of six multi values are allowed for this field.

        Parameters:
        param - the AsInterestDet to append
        pos - The position where to insert the value.

      • insertEntryIds

        public void insertEntryIds(java.lang.CharSequence param, int pos)
        Insert the specified EntryIds to the specified position in the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Multi-valued field which identifies the entries raised by the contract. The entry Ids are generated automatically by the system and identify either a statement entry or a category entry in respect of the contract. The number automatically generated is unique to the associated contract and is built in the following way : Eg. 673732684.48 o The first four digits "6737" indicates the number of days since the 1st of January 1968. o The next five "32684" indicates the number of seconds since midnight. o The last two digits "48" indicates the number of hundreds of seconds. Validation Rules: 29 Alphanumeric characters. (No-input. System generated).

        Parameters:
        param - the EntryIds to append
        pos - The position where to insert the value.
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setActionType

        public void setActionType(TField value)
        Set the specified value for ActionType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository. Under the Regulatory Reporting to a Trade Repository, it is not only the initial trade that is reported but also the life cycle events of the Trade that follow. A change in the action type is indicative of an event on the contract and requires to be reported. Change in Action Types is allowed both manually and automatically. Specifies the ACTION.TYPE that is populated based on the event on trade. Input to this field is allowed only when OC module is installed. Validation Rules: Allowed optional values are N, M, E, C, Z, O, R and P N denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is NEW. Value of 'N' is defaulted for a new contract. User is also allowed to change the status to N if the previous status is E. E denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is REVERSE or Correction. In case of wrongly entered UTI values or a Temporary UTI was used previously, the old UTI should be reported with ACTION.TYPE as 'E' for error reporting first and then change the Action Type to NEW after keying in the actual UTI. This way the previous reporting with temporary UTI is replaced by the one with final UTI. Action Type E is also used to undo the reporting of a particular transaction done which should not have been done reported at all in the first instance. M denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is MODIFIED. In case of change in the RATE.FIXING.DATE the ACTION.TYPE is set to 'M'. C denotes that the ACTION.TYPE is CANCELLED. In case of any change in maturity/value date i.e. early termination of the contract should be reported with C. In FRA this MATURITY.DATE field is No change field. So ACTION.TYPE never gets populated automatically with type as C but It can be manually updated as c and the contract can be cancelled. Z denotes Compression update. This means the trade being reported is generated out of a compression activity. O denotes OTHER types. When OTHER is used, additional information as to what OTHER mean should be mentioned separately.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setAgreementType(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AgreementType
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the swap contract Agreement type. If a matster agreement type is entered then the default full agreement type (eg TYPE / DATE // VERSION) will be used on the SWAP contract if such an agreement type has been entered on the master SWAP.AGREEMENT.TYPE record. Eg. ISDA (International Swap Dealers Association), BBAIRS, MASTER, etc. This is also used to define Swift Message conditions. Corresponds to field 77 on Swift messages. Validation Rules: 1-12 Alphanumeric characters. (Mandatory input). Must be a valid definition on the SWAP.AGREEMENT.TYPE file. Each contract must be linked to an agreement type.

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Interest Day Basis which indicates the calculation method to be used for interest amount calculations on the asset leg. Input can be any valid basis type defined on the INTEREST.BASIS table. Eg. Basis Calculation method signified ===== ============================ A 360/360 A2 30/360 B 366/360 C Act/Act (ISDA) C2 Act/Act (AFB) D 360/366 E 366/365 E1 365/365 F 360/365 F2 30/365 S SPECIAL Validation Rules: 1-10 Alphanumeric characters. (Mandatory input). The Basis type entered must be a valid key on the INTEREST.BASIS table. Defaulted to the Interest Day Basis specified on the CURRENCY file for the Asset currency (AS.CURRENCY). For Basis type 'S' the INTEREST amount will be Mandatory. Also FIXED.RATE and RATE.KEY are not allowed.

      • setAsDateAdjustment

        public void setAsDateAdjustment(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AsDateAdjustment
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the type of date adjustments that are to be followed on the Asset leg. Depending on the date adjustment, the process date of the schedules and the interest effective dates are calculated. Valid date adjustments and their effects are as follows : DATE.ADJUSTMENT ENTRY.DATE EFFECTIVE.DATE =============== ========== ============== o null SCHEDULE.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o VALUE PROCESS.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o PERIOD PROCESS.DATE PROCESS.DATE Where, ENTRY.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Date Adjustment specified (AS.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). EFFECTIVE.DATE is the end date of the current interest period determined by the Date Adjustment specified (AS.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). SCHEDULE.DATE is the date of the schedule as specified in the swap contract (AS.DATE.FREQ). PROCESS.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Asset Day Convention (AS.DAY.CONVENTION). Validation Rules: 1-6 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Must be set to either "null", "VALUE", or "PERIOD".

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setAsDayConvention

        public void setAsDayConvention(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AsDayConvention
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Day Convention to follow. Based on the Day Convention (AS.DAY.CONVENTION) and the Business Centres (AS.BUS.CENTRES) the process date of the Asset leg schedules are determined. Valid Day Conventions are as follows : o null the process date is the date of the schedule. o FOLLOWING the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule. o MODIFIED the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule providing this date does not fall into the next calendar month. In which case the process date is the first preceding business day. o PRECEDING the process date is the first preceding business day. Validation Rules: 1-10 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Valid Day Conventions are either "null", "FOLLOWING", "PRECEDING", or "MODIFIED".

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setAsFixedInterest(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for AsFixedInterest
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies whether the current interest amount payments on the asset leg are of a fixed or floating amount. This field is a no-input field and is set to either "Y" for fixed interest amounts, and "NO" (default) for floating interest amounts. This field is determined by the interest payment schedules ("IP") defined on the Asset side of the contract. o If the IP schedule (AS.TYPE) has an amount specified (AS.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "Y". o If the IP schedule (AS.TYPE) does not have an amount specified (AS.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "NO". Validation Rules: 1-2 Alpha characters. "Y" signifies a fixed interest amount for the current period. "NO" signifies a floating interest amount for the current period. (No-input field. Default = "NO").

        public void setAsIntEffective(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AsIntEffective
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the start date of the first interest period and therefore the true Value date of the Asset leg. It is the date on which interest accruals commence on the outstanding balance of the contract. This date can be entered as either the current date (today) or a date in the past (less than the contract value date). It cannot be greater than the contract value date. If forward dated, ie. both the value date and interest effective date are forward, then the contract status will be null until the effective date is reached, at which time, the principal amount will be drawn down and the contract status changed to "CUR". An input of a null value will result in the date being defaulted to the contract value date. If backdated or 'today' dated then the contract will be drawn down, put on-line, and the contract status set to "CUR". If backdated into a prior month, interest will be accrued on-line up to the end of the previous month. Input of a non working day will require an override. Validation Rules: Standard Date format. Defaults to the contract Value Date. Cannot be greater than the contract Value Date. Input is prohibited was the contract status has been set to "CUR" (Current). An override will be required if this date is a non-working day.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setAsInterestDet

        public void setAsInterestDet(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)
        Set the specified AsInterestDet to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The interest details of the asset leg of the swap transaction are stored here. This field will only be used when the assest leg is floating, and is used when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record does not hold sufficient detail for the generation of the SWIFT message. In this case the value 'OTHER' is used in field 14F on the SWIFT message and the value in this field is used. This field will not be used if the asset leg is fixed. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record specified in the field AS.RATE.KEY has a rate text which does not correspond to the format alpha / alpha / alpha. Refer to the helptext on field RATE.TEXT on the file MARKET.RATE.TEXT A maximum of six multi values are allowed for this field.

        public void setAsPrincipal(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AsPrincipal
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The Principal amount of the Asset side of the swap contract which will always be expressed in the currency defined in the previous field. In order to facilitate the efficient entry of the amount, an input feature has been provided which allows for the suppression of trailing zeros. In English Language text this is accomplished by using a 'T' to indicate the thousands and an 'M' to indicate the millions. Other languages will require the provision of translation values. E.g. INPUT VALUE 1T 1,000.00 2M 2,000,000.00 Validation Rules: 1-19 type AMT (standard amount format) characters plus a decimal point. (Mandatory input) The amount must be greater than Zero.

      • setAsSpread

        public void setAsSpread(TField value)
        Set the specified value for AsSpread
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates the spread (also known as the margin) which will be applied to the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. Note: T24 allows the user to define, on Floating rate contracts, a spread which can be added to or subtracted from the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. The subtraction of the INTEREST SPREAD from the INTEREST KEY must be specifically indicated by the insertion of the '-' (minus) sign in front of the INTEREST SPREAD. Validation Rules: Upto 11 numeric characters plus a decimal point. A minus sign has to be placed in front if the spread is to be deducted from the INTEREST KEY. Input is optional when a rate key has been define, ie. AS.RATE.KEY, otherwise input is not allowed. (Default value = null) Input in this field is only allowed for contracts when a rate key has been specified, ie. AS.RATE.KEY is not null.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

A rate must be present in this field if the fields AS.RATE.KEY and AS.SPREAD are null. Field will be no-input once the contract has reached the Interest effective date, ie. contract status = "CUR".

      • setBalanceSheet

        public void setBalanceSheet(TField value)
        Set the specified value for BalanceSheet
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field details whether the SWAP contract is to be treated as an ON balance sheet instrument or an OFF balance sheet instrument. This value is defaulted from the SWAP.TYPE of the swap contract. When this field contains the value OFF the contract will undergo the currency revaluation processing. Each night each leg of the contract id revalued against the local currency if 1) The leg is not notional (ie the NOTIONAL field on the SWAP.BALANCES file is set to NO). 2) The currency of the leg is not the local currency. And any difference between this value and the value as of last night is posted as unreleasied profit and loss to the category specified on the SWAP.PARAMETER record. When this field contains the value of ON the contract will not be revalued. Validation Rules: Must contain either ON or OFF, which is set from the SWAP.TYPE. Input is not allowed to this field.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

      • setBaseCurrency

        public void setBaseCurrency(TField value)
        Set the specified value for BaseCurrency
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the base currency of the contract and will be used to verify the exchange rate. When the Base Currency is not specified and the transaction involves local Currency, the System will default to the local Currency provided that the Quotation code of the other Currency is NULL. If this is not the case (the Quotation code of the other Currency is not equal to null) then the other Currency will become the default. When the base Currency is not specified and the transaction involves two currencies where none is the Local Currency, it will default to the Currency which yields a cross-rate greater than unity (One). Please refer to Forex for more details. Validation Rules: 3 characters currency code (uppercase alpha or numeric) - Type SSS (Optional input. See details for default.) The currency entered must appear on the Currency table. The currency must be the same as either the asset or liability currency. Proper verification of the exchange rate will be performed by the system against the Exchange Rate values contained in the Currency table. When the Swap contract involves the local currency and the quotation code on the Foreign currency is equal to or greater than '0' (zero), the base currency can only be the Foreign Currency. Once authorised the Base currency cannot be amended.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCurrencyMarket

        public void setCurrencyMarket(TField value)
        Set the specified value for CurrencyMarket
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies which Currency Market is accessed for this transaction. The use of this field will only be applicable for those countries where the exchange authorities have defined different markets for foreign currency dealing. A typical example would be Belgium where foreign currencies are dealt with on the Regular Market and also on the Free Market. The default value of '1' means that, for the majority of countries, where only one exchange rate market exists, input in this field will not be necessary. Note: In the present release, only one market can be defined on the CURRENCY.MARKET table. Consequently, for the time being, only the value of '1' will be accepted in this field. Validation Rules: One Numeric digit Currency Market code. (No input. System value is 1.) Any input in this field must be a valid code on the CURRENCY.MARKET table.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setCustomer

        public void setCustomer(TField value)
        Set the specified value for Customer
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the counterparty with whom the Bank makes the contract. This is the identification assigned to the Customer on first contact with the bank. The customer will be referred to by this identification in all subsequent operations with the Bank. The system will make use of this number to: a) Identify the Counterparty of the transaction engaged in by the Bank, b) Print the Customer's name and address on all contracts and/or advices produced by this module, c) Locate the liability number for limit checking on Placement contracts. Validation Rules: 3-10 alphanumeric customer mnemonic or, 1-10 numeric character customer number. (Mandatory input). Must be a valid Customer number or mnemonic. Once the contract has been authorised, this field cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setEntryIds

        public void setEntryIds(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)
        Set the specified EntryIds to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Multi-valued field which identifies the entries raised by the contract. The entry Ids are generated automatically by the system and identify either a statement entry or a category entry in respect of the contract. The number automatically generated is unique to the associated contract and is built in the following way : Eg. 673732684.48 o The first four digits "6737" indicates the number of days since the 1st of January 1968. o The next five "32684" indicates the number of seconds since midnight. o The last two digits "48" indicates the number of hundreds of seconds. Validation Rules: 29 Alphanumeric characters. (No-input. System generated).

        Parameters:
        param - the EntryIds to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setFttCollCptyTax

        public void setFttCollCptyTax(TField value)
        Set the specified value for FttCollCptyTax
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Provides the option to T24 bank to collect the Financial Transaction Tax payable by the Counterparty also. If yes, accounting entries are raised to collect counterpartys tax wherein customer Account is debited and Tax suspense Account is credited. The values No or Null means T24 bank does not collect the FTT payable by the counterparty or in other words the counterparty himself remits the FTT. This option is provided on the premise that where the counterparty is a customer of the bank ( not an interbank counterparty) the T24 bank assumes responsibility to collect and pay the FTT payable by the customer Validation Rules: Values allowed are Yes, No or Null. Default value will be from SWAP.PARAMETER but can be overridden by the User.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setFttTaxBaseCcy

        Set the specified value for FttTaxBaseCcy
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the Tax Base Currency in which Tax amount is calculated. 1. In Single currency Swaps, the currency of the swap is considered as the tax base currency and the principal notional amount becomes the tax base amount. 2. In Cross currency swaps, if EUR is present in either of the legs then EUR, else the higher of the two currencies in terms of local currency value will be the Tax base ccy and its corresponding amount as tax base amount. Validation Rules : Can be one of the currency of transaction currency pairs No Change field after authorization. Associated with TAX.BASE.AMT

      • setFwdRateKey

        public void setFwdRateKey(TField value)
        Set the specified value for FwdRateKey
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates the PI Rate key to be used to derive the implicit future/ forward rate for calculating the future cash flows of Floating Leg as part of NPV revaluation process. Default value will be from FWD.RATE.KEY of SWAP.REVAL.PARAMETER, if defined. When a rate key is defined/defaulted, the implicit future/forward rates are derived from the given rate curve. When the field is left blank, the forward rate is derived using As.Rate.key / Lb.Rate.key curve for Asset / Liability leg respectively.

        Even as the zero rates / implied spot rates are obtained from market data sources for the purpose of discounting the cash flows, the same PI key can be applied on this field for deriving the implicit forward rates.

        Validation Rules: Must be a valid rate key defined in PERIODIC.INTEREST table for Asset / Liability currencies. Valid rate key range are 01 to 99.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

Input can be any valid basis type defined on the INTEREST.BASIS table. Eg. Basis Calculation method signified ===== ============================ A 360/360 A2 30/360 B 366/360 C Act/Act (ISDA) C2 Act/Act (AFB) 366/366 for leap years D 360/366 E 366/365 E1 365/365 F 360/365 F2 30/365 S SPECIAL Validation Rules: 1-10 Alphanumeric characters. (Mandatory input). The Basis type entered must be a valid key on the INTEREST.BASIS table. Defaulted to the Interest Day Basis specified on the CURRENCY file for the Liability currency (LB.CURRENCY). For Basis type 'S' the INTEREST amount will be Mandatory. Also FIXED.RATE and RATE.KEY are not allowed.

        public void setLbCurrency(TField value)
        Set the specified value for LbCurrency
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates the currency of the liability side of the swap contract. This field indicates the currency of the liability side of the swap contract and will be the same as the currency of the various accounts where the accounting movements in respect of the contract will be debited or credited. Validation Rules: 3 type SSS (uppercase alpha) characters. or 1-3 numeric character currency code. (Optional input; Default = Asset currency). The currency code must exist on the CURRENCY table. Any existing currency code will be accepted and the name redisplayed for checking. Defaults to the currency defined on the Asset leg (AS.CURRENCY). Once the contract has been authorised this field cannot be changed.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

This field is a no-input field and is defaulted via : o The fixed interest rate (LB.FIXED.RATE) or, o The combined/calculated floating interest rate using LB.RATE.KEY and LB.SPREAD This rate can only be changed by defining and processing a Rate Reset schedule (type "RR") on the contract. Validation Rules: 1-11 numeric characters. (No-input field). If the current rate is not greater than zero, an override message is set.

      • setLbDateAdjustment

        public void setLbDateAdjustment(TField value)
        Set the specified value for LbDateAdjustment
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the type of date adjustments that are to be followed on the Liability leg. Depending on the date adjustment, the process date of the schedules and the interest effective dates are calculated. Valid date adjustments and their effects are as follows : DATE.ADJUSTMENT ENTRY.DATE EFFECTIVE.DATE =============== ========== ============== o null SCHEDULE.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o VALUE PROCESS.DATE SCHEDULE.DATE o PERIOD PROCESS.DATE PROCESS.DATE Where, ENTRY.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Date Adjustment specified (LB.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). EFFECTIVE.DATE is the end date of the current interest period determined by the Date Adjustment specified (LB.DATE.ADJUSTMENT). SCHEDULE.DATE is the date of the schedule as specified in the swap contract (LB.DATE.FREQ). PROCESS.DATE is the process date of the schedule determined by the Asset Day Convention (LB.DAY.CONVENTION). Validation Rules: 1-6 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Must be set to either "null", "VALUE", or "PERIOD".

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setLbDayConvention

        public void setLbDayConvention(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for LbDayConvention
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Day Convention to follow. Based on the Day Convention (LB.DAY.CONVENTION) and the Business Centres (LB.BUS.CENTRES) the process date of the Liability leg schedules are determined. Valid Day Conventions are as follows : o null the process date is the date of the schedule. o FOLLOWING the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule. o MODIFIED the process date is the next business day after the date of the schedule providing this date does not fall into the next calendar month. In which case the process date is the first preceding business day. o PRECEDING the process date is the first preceding business day. Validation Rules: 1-10 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input. Default = null). Valid Day Conventions are either "null", "FOLLOWING", "PRECEDING", or "MODIFIED".

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setLbFixedInterest

        public void setLbFixedInterest(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for LbFixedInterest
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies whether the current interest amount payments on the liability leg are of a fixed or floating amount. This field is a no-input field and is set to either "Y" for fixed interest amounts, and "NO" (default) for floating interest amounts. This field is determined by the interest payment schedules ("IP") defined on the Asset side of the contract. o If the IP schedule (LB.TYPE) has an amount specified (LB.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "Y". o If the IP schedule (LB.TYPE) does not have an amount specified (LB.AMOUNT) then fixed interest is "NO". Validation Rules: 1-2 Alpha characters. "Y" signifies a fixed interest amount for the current period. "NO" signifies a floating interest amount for the current period. (No-input field. Default = "NO").

      • setLbIntEffective

        public void setLbIntEffective(TField value)
        Set the specified value for LbIntEffective
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the start date of the first interest period and therefore the true Value date of the Liability leg. It is the date on which interest accruals commence on the outstanding balance of the contract. This date can be entered as either the current date (today) or a date in the past (less than the contract value date). It cannot be greater than the contract value date. If forward dated, ie. both the value date and interest effective date are forward, then the contract status will be null until the effective date is reached, at which time, the principal amount will be drawn down and the contract status changed to "CUR". An input of a null value will result in the date being defaulted to the contract value date. If backdated or 'today' dated then the contract will be drawn down, put on-line, and the contract status set to "CUR". If backdated into a prior month, interest will be accrued on-line up to the end of the previous month. Input of a non working day will require an override. Validation Rules: Standard Date format. Defaults to the contract Value Date. Cannot be greater than the contract Value Date. Input is prohibited was the contract status has been set to "CUR" (Current). An override will be required if this date is a non-working day.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Set the specified LbInterestDet to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The interest details of the liability leg of the swap transaction are stored here. This field will only be used when the liability leg is floating, and is used when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record does not hold sufficient detail for the generation of the SWIFT message. Validation Rules: Mandatory Input when the MARKET.RATE.TEXT record specified in the field LB.RATE.KEY has a rate text which does not correspond to the format alpha / alpha / alpha. Refer to the helptext on field RATE.TEXT on the file MARKET.RATE.TEXT A maximum of six multi values are allowed for this field.

        Field description: The Principal amount of the Liability side of the swap contract which will always be expressed in the currency defined in the previous field. In English Language text this is accomplished by using a 'T' to indicate the thousands and an 'M' to indicate the millions. Other languages will require the provision of translation values. E.g. INPUT VALUE 1T 1,000.00 2M 2,000,000.00 Validation Rules: 1-19 type AMT (standard amount format) characters plus a decimal point. (Mandatory input) The amount must be greater than Zero. Defaults to the principal amount defined on the Asset leg (AS.PRINCIPAL).

      • setLbSpread

        public void setLbSpread(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for LbSpread
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Indicates the spread (also known as the margin) which will be applied to the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. Note : T24 allows the user to define, on Floating rate contracts, a spread which can be added to or subtracted from the percentage interest rate related to the INTEREST KEY. The subtraction of the INTEREST SPREAD from the INTEREST KEY must be specifically indicated by the insertion of the '-' (minus) sign in front of the INTEREST SPREAD. Validation Rules: Upto 11 numeric characters plus a decimal point. A minus sign has to be placed in front if the spread is to be deducted from the INTEREST KEY. Input is optional when a rate key has been define, ie. LB.RATE.KEY, otherwise input is not allowed. (Default value = null) Input in this field is only allowed for contracts when a rate key has been specified, ie. LB.RATE.KEY is not null.

        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies the LIMIT REFERENCE number to be checked for Limit control on transactions. Specifies the Credit Line number under which the transaction was granted. If no input is made in this field, then the Limits system will provide a default value according to the Limit Reference record which has its field application identifier set tyo "SW". If no match is found in selective Reference, the default value will be the Reference with its field reference blank. The credit line number generated will be NNNN-01 where NNNN is the Id of the Limit Reference record described above. Validation Rules: 3 - 10 numeric character LIMIT REFERENCE code. (Optional Input. Default value). Input in this field must be a valid LIMIT REFERENCE number. If no Limit exists for the counterparty a corresponding error message will be displayed by the system with an override facility. If the transaction amount exceeds the availability amount of the Limit, a corresponding error message will be displayed with an override facility.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setLinkReference

        public void setLinkReference(TField value)
        Set the specified value for LinkReference
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Defines the Transaction link reference of the Swap contract. The TRANS.LINK.REFERENCE file enables transactions to be linked together for reporting purposes. Eg. A Swap contract to a backing Loans and Deposits contract. The updating of the file is fully automatic : o If the user enters a reference id that does not exist on the reference file, a new record is created, and the contract Id concerned is held. o If the user changes the reference id, the contract Id concerned is moved to the new reference record. Should no other contracts exist on the reference, then that reference is removed. Validation Rules: 1-12 Alpha-numeric characters. (Optional input).

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setLiquidationMode

        public void setLiquidationMode(TField value)
        Set the specified value for LiquidationMode
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field identifies the manner in which overdue payments are handled. The default for all contracts is AUTOMATIC. There are three options available: AUTOMATIC SEMI-AUTOMATIC MANUAL AUTOMATIC will liquidate across the settlement accounts on the contract. MANUAL will create a PD contract instead. SEMI-AUTOMATIC will only raise a PD contract if insufficient funds exist on the settlement account. For further details see the helptext in PD.PARAMETER where these settings are controlled from. Validation Rules: If the PD product is not installed for the current company then the only allowed setting is AUTOMATIC. Only AUTOMATIC allowed for liability contract types.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setMatPaymentDate

        public void setMatPaymentDate(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for MatPaymentDate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies whether the value date (Payment date) for the schedules that fall on the maturity date should be updated with the next working day of the deal currency when the maturity date of the Swap contract is a holiday. This functionality will be applicable only for the schedules that fall on the maturity date, provided DAY.CONVENTION is set as Following/ Modified. In case of Modified, if the last day of the month is a non-working day, then the value date will be the previous working day (as per PRECEDING). Irrespective of the input given in the field DATE.ADJUSTMENT (PERIOD or VALUE), System treats this as VALUE for the schedules falling on the maturity date, when the DAY.CONVENTION is set as Following/ Modified (excepting month end scenario). The new functionality of populating the value date will be applicable only when the field is set to YES. Validation Rules: : Input in this field is allowed only when the field MAT.PAYMENT.DATE in SWAP.PARAMETER is set to 'YES'. 'YES','NO' and NONE are the proposed values This field will be defaulted to YES if the field MAT.PAYMENT.DATE in SWAP.PARAMETER is set to 'YES' No input field after first authorisation

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setMaturityDate

        public void setMaturityDate(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for MaturityDate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Identifies when the swap contract is due to terminate. This field represents the latter date of when the principals are re-exchanged as scheduled, (AS/LB.TYPE = RX,CM) or when the final interest payment is made. The asset and liability dates for the re-exchange of principals or interest payments may not always be the same. The Maturity Date is the date on which the deal will be liquidated. At liquidation, all the corresponding amounts of principal (if appropriate) and interest will be passed to the appropriate accounts as designated within the transaction. Validation Rules: Type DD (standard date format in range 1000 - 2049) or, 3 numeric characters representing a number of days: (Mandatory input) The date will be checked against the HOLIDAY table. Any non-working day will require an override prior to acceptance. The maturity date must be greater than the value date. This date cannot be changed after authorisation when INTEREST BASIS = 'S' (Special). For Asset type contract, an override will be required when this date is smaller than the EXPIRY DATE of the corresponding Credit line.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing
