      • setOcClgStatus

        public void setOcClgStatus(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for OcClgStatus
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository. Denotes the OC Clearing Status. Input to this field is allowed only when OC module is installed. Validation Rules: Allowed optional values are Bilateral, Submitted, Accepted, Rejected, Cleared and Terminated. BILATERAL - when a fresh contract is inputted this field should be updated as BILATERAL. The previous status should be null. SUBMITTED - when the inputted contract is submitted to Trade Repository it should get updated as SUBMITTED.The previous clearing status of the contract should be BILATERAL. when OC.CLG.STATUS of the contract is SUBMITTED both CLG.MEM.ID and CENTRAl.CLG.PARTY fields cannot be NULL. ACCEPTED - when the contract is accepted by the Trade Repository it should get updated as ACCEPTED.The previous status should be SUBMITTED REJECTED - when the contract is rejected by the Trade Repository it should get updated as REJECTED.The previous status should be SUBMITTED CLEARED - When the status of the contract is ACCEPTED, User is expected to reverse the contract and enter a new one with Trade status as CLEARED.When the status is CLEARED, fields like CENTRAL.CLG.PARTY, CLG.MEM.ID, BILATERAL.REF are mandatory. Terminated - A cleared contract when cancelled/terminated by the Trade Repository should be updated as TERMINATED.The previous status should be CLEARED. This is a no change field.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setTreasuryCustomer

        public void setTreasuryCustomer(TField value)
        Set the specified value for TreasuryCustomer
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: The field will either hold values NULL or NO. By default it will hold NULL value, meaning that the customer in the deal is a treasury customer. It can be set to NO at the input level, wherein the interest rate charged to the customer is different from the treasury interest rate. Once this field is set to NO, then it becomes mandatory to input the treasury interest rate in the asset or liability side or both. When both the asset and liability side interest rate is set to floating, then TREASURY.CUSTOMER cannot be set to NO.The value in the field cannot be changed from NULL to NO or vice versa after authorization of the SWAP contract. The following input will be allowed in this field: 'NULL' = which means that the CPARTYof the deal is a Treasury Customer. 'NO' = which means that the CPARTYof the deal is not a Treasury Customer. (Optional input; default value = Null, i.e. the CPARTY is a Treasury Customer.)

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUniTranId

        public void setUniTranId(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for UniTranId
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository All Trades should have a Unique Transaction Identifier (UTI) which is generated, communicated and matched Determination of who generates the UTI should follow the existing industry best practices for that Asset class The UTI.USI.API attached in OC.PARAMETER and invoked during FRA deal capture determines who is the party responsible for UTI generation and does the following. If a value is present during deal capture the API is not invoked, on the assumption that the UTI is generated and supplied by the other Counterparty. If no value is present during the deal capture, the API is invoked to determine the party responsible for generating the UTI. If the Other counterparty is responsible, still an UTI is generated with a suffix as TEMP to show that the UTI from the other counterparty is awaited and in the meantime, the reporting is done with a Temporary ID. If T24 Bank is responsible for UTI generation, then the same is generated without TEMP. Where a reporting has been made with UTI having TEMP as suffix and subsequently the Counterparty supplies the UTI, the following procedure has to be followed to ensure reporting with actual UTI. The field Action Type needs to be changed to E and record to be authorized. Later, the UTI field should be modified with the actual UTI received. Set the Action Type field to N and authorize the record. In this way, the previous reporting gets cancelled and the new reporting goes with correct UTI. Input to this field is allowed only when OC module is installed. Validation Rules : can contain up to 52 alphanumeric characters

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUniTranId

        public void setUniTranId(TField value)
        Set the specified value for UniTranId
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Part of Regulatory Reporting information to a Trade Repository All Trades should have a Unique Transaction Identifier (UTI) which is generated, communicated and matched Determination of who generates the UTI should follow the existing industry best practices for that Asset class The UTI.USI.API attached in OC.PARAMETER and invoked during FRA deal capture determines who is the party responsible for UTI generation and does the following.       • setValueDate

        public void setValueDate(TField value)
        Set the specified value for ValueDate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Contains the value date of the contract and is therefore the date from which the system will start to accrue interest. This date must be prior to the Maturity Date of the Contract such that the system may calculate interest. Validation Rules: Type DD (standard date format in range 1000 - 2049). (Optional input; Default value = Run date). The system will automatically access the HOLIDAY table to ensure that the value date is a working day and not a holiday in the country associated to the currency of the contract. Any Holiday will require an override.

        nothing

      • setVariationMarginPosted

        public void setVariationMarginPosted(TField value)
        Set the specified value for VariationMarginPosted
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field holds the Value of the variation margin posted, including cash settled, by the reporting counterparty to the other counterparty. Where variation margin is posted on a portfolio basis, this field would indicate the overall value of variation margin posted for the portfolio. Validation Rules: Field is inputtable only if OC module is enabled

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing
